msg:Typically all counter staffs are able to communicate in English and polite. 
Must give the biggest credit to their housekeeping staffs who done a wonderful job daily for changing the linens and cleaning. This is the best part of their strength. 
Breakfast is alright nothing to shout for. Very simple local and international food. In fact quite limited. 
Room is spacious, aircon is working well but wifi really slow and somehow hang. Even their TV sometimes went without signal. For people who relied very much on the wifi for their work, you would be facing laggy downloading. 
Location wise, not too bad. There is a local Szechuan restaurant that opened till 2am just beside the hotel which served very good food. There is a Carrefour but only using phone payment. Starbucks, other cafe just few steps away as well as 24hours family mart. There is a Cantonese restaurant serving good roast meat and some fast food and ice cream chain could be found. If still unhappy, can go across the street for Laya Mall though mainly for children enrichment centers.
